   akṣayairasamairyukto guṇairlokeṣu dṛśyase /	akzayEH asamEH yuktaH guNEH lokezu dRSyase /
   maṇḍaleṣvapyadṛśyaśca sarvathā devamānuṣaiḥ // MSA_20.61 //	maNxalezu api adRSyaH ca sarvaTA deva mAnuzEH // MSAH _20.61 //
   mahāyānasūtrālaṃkāreṣu vyavadātasamayamahābodhisatvabhāṣite	mahAyAna sUtra alaMkArezu vyavadAta samaya mahA boDisatva BAzite
   caryāpratiṣṭhādhikāro nāmaikaviṃśatitamo 'dhikāraḥ	caryApratizWA aDikAraH nAma ekaviMSatitamaH aDikAraH
   samāptaśca mahāyānasūtrālaṃkāra iti	samAptaH ca mahAyAna sUtra alaMkAraH iti
